### [224] [Learning Constraints from Stochastic Partially-Observed Closed-Loop Demonstrations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.15109)
*Chih-Yuan Chiu,Zhouyu Zhang,Glen Chou*

Main category: eess.SY

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种算法，用于从局部最优的输入-输出轨迹数据中学习未知的参数化约束，这些数据由具有随机非线性动力学且执行鲁棒反馈控制以满足约束的演示者生成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究的动机是，演示者通过状态或输出反馈控制来鲁棒地满足约束，即使存在最坏情况的动力学和输出噪声。目标是从这些演示数据中学习他们所遵循的未知约束。

Method: 该方法将鲁棒最优输出反馈控制问题的Karush-Kuhn-Tucker (KKT) 条件编码为一个可行性问题，以恢复与演示的局部最优性一致的约束。

Result: 该约束学习方法能够：(i) 准确恢复演示者的状态或输出反馈策略；(ii) 保守估计所有在最坏情况噪声下确保约束满足的状态或输出反馈策略集合。此外，当演示数据被传输错误破坏时，学习到的状态或输出反馈律的不准确性与错误幅度呈线性关系。该方法能准确地从模拟的、带噪声的闭环演示中恢复未知约束，适用于线性和非线性动力学（如独轮车和四旋翼），以及各种状态和输出反馈机制。

Conclusion: 该算法能够准确地从噪声、闭环演示数据中恢复未知的参数化约束和相应的反馈策略，并且对传输错误具有可量化的鲁棒性，适用于多种动态系统和反馈机制。

Abstract: We present an algorithm for learning unknown parametric constraints from
locally-optimal input-output trajectory data. We assume that the given data is
generated by demonstrators with stochastic nonlinear dynamics who execute a
state or output feedback law to robustly satisfy the constraints despite
worst-case dynamics and output noise. We encode the Karush-Kuhn-Tucker (KKT)
conditions of this robust optimal output feedback control problem within a
feasibility problem to recover constraints consistent with the local optimality
of the demonstrations. We prove that our constraint learning method (i)
accurately recovers the demonstrator's state or output feedback policy, and
(ii) conservatively estimates the set of all state or output feedback policies
that ensure constraint satisfaction despite worst-case noise realizations.
Moreover, we perform sensitivity analysis, proving that when demonstrations are
corrupted by transmission error, the inaccuracy in the learned state or output
feedback law scales linearly in the error magnitude. Our method accurately
recovers unknown constraints from simulated noisy, closed-loop demonstrations
generated using dynamics, both linear and nonlinear, (e.g., unicycle and
quadrotor) and a range of state and output feedback mechanisms.

*Lohitvel Gopikannan,Shashi Ranjan Kumar,Abhinav Sinha*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1. 采用固定时间分布式观测器，使无导引头的拦截器能通过有导引头拦截器和邻居信息估计目标状态。2. 利用偏离追逐制导（deviated pursuit guidance）获得精确的剩余飞行时间表达式。3. 运用高阶滑模共识协议，在有限时间内实现剩余飞行时间共识。

Abstract: This paper presents a cooperative guidance strategy for the simultaneous

seeker-equipped agents and local neighbors over a directed communication
topology. Departing from conventional strategies that approximate time-to-go
via linearization or small-angle assumptions, the proposed approach leverages
deviated pursuit guidance where the time-to-go expression is exact for such a
target. Moreover, a higher-order sliding mode consensus protocol is utilized to
establish time-to-go consensus within a finite time. The effectiveness of the

simulations.

### [226] [D4PM: A Dual-branch Driven Denoising Diffusion Probabilistic Model with Joint Posterior Diffusion Sampling for EEG Artifacts Removal](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.14302)
*Feixue Shao,Xueyu Liu,Yongfei Wu,Jianbo Lu,Guiying Yan,Weihua Yang*

Main category: eess.IV

TL;DR: 本文提出了D4PM，一个双分支驱动的去噪扩散概率模型，旨在统一多种EEG伪影的去除。该模型通过双分支条件扩散架构隐式建模干净EEG和伪影的数据分布，并设计了联合后验采样策略以实现高保真重建。实验证明D4PM在去噪方面表现优越，并在EOG伪影去除上达到了新的最先进水平。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: EEG信号中的伪影去除对准确分析至关重要。传统方法在伪影与EEG强相关或单通道数据下表现不佳。尽管扩散模型在EEG去噪中显示出潜力，但现有方法存在两个主要限制：缺乏时间建模（限制可解释性）和单一伪影训练范式（忽略伪影间差异）。

Method: 本文提出D4PM，一个双分支驱动的去噪扩散概率模型，用于统一多类型伪影去除。D4PM引入了双分支条件扩散架构来隐式建模干净EEG和伪影的数据分布。此外，还设计了一种联合后验采样策略，以协同整合互补先验，从而实现高保真EEG重建。

Result: 在两个公共数据集上进行的广泛实验表明，D4PM提供了卓越的去噪性能。它在EOG伪影去除方面取得了新的最先进（SOTA）性能，超越了所有公开可用的基线方法。

Conclusion: D4PM通过其创新的双分支条件扩散架构和联合后验采样策略，有效地解决了现有扩散模型在EEG伪影去除中的局限性，实现了多类型伪影的统一去除，并在EOG伪影去除上树立了新的性能标杆。

Abstract: Artifact removal is critical for accurate analysis and interpretation of
Electroencephalogram (EEG) signals. Traditional methods perform poorly with
strong artifact-EEG correlations or single-channel data. Recent advances in
diffusion-based generative models have demonstrated strong potential for EEG
denoising, notably improving fine-grained noise suppression and reducing
over-smoothing. However, existing methods face two main limitations: lack of
temporal modeling limits interpretability and the use of single-artifact
training paradigms ignore inter-artifact differences. To address these issues,
we propose D4PM, a dual-branch driven denoising diffusion probabilistic model
that unifies multi-type artifact removal. We introduce a dual-branch
conditional diffusion architecture to implicitly model the data distribution of
clean EEG and artifacts. A joint posterior sampling strategy is further
designed to collaboratively integrate complementary priors for high-fidelity
EEG reconstruction. Extensive experiments on two public datasets show that D4PM
delivers superior denoising. It achieves new state-of-the-art performance in
EOG artifact removal, outperforming all publicly available baselines. The code
is available at https://github.com/flysnow1024/D4PM.

</details>


### [227] [UTOPY: Unrolling Algorithm Learning via Fidelity Homotopy for Inverse Problems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.14394)
*Roman Jacome,Romario Gualdrón-Hurtado,Leon Suarez-Rodriguez,Henry Arguello*

Main category: eess.IV

TL;DR: 针对成像逆问题中高度病态感知算子导致的展开算法性能下降问题，本文提出UTOPY，一种基于同伦连续的训练方法。它通过从一个良好病态的合成感知矩阵平滑过渡到目标病态问题，显著提高了重建质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 展开算法因其可解释性和高精度在成像逆问题重建中广受欢迎。然而，当感知算子高度病态时，数据保真项上的梯度步长会阻碍收敛并降低重建质量。

Method: 本文提出了UTOPY，一种用于训练展开算法的同伦连续公式。该方法在展开网络优化初期使用一个良好病态（合成）的感知矩阵，并定义了一个连续路径策略，以平滑地从合成保真度过渡到所需的病态问题，使网络能够逐步从简单问题过渡到更具挑战性的目标场景。

Result: 理论上，对于投影梯度下降类展开模型，所提出的连续策略生成了展开解的平滑路径。在压缩感知和图像去模糊实验中，该方法始终优于传统的展开训练，重建性能最高可提高2.5 dB PSNR。

Conclusion: UTOPY通过引入同伦连续训练策略，有效解决了展开算法在处理高度病态感知算子时的收敛和重建质量问题，显著提升了图像重建性能。

Abstract: Imaging Inverse problems aim to reconstruct an underlying image from
undersampled, coded, and noisy observations. Within the wide range of
reconstruction frameworks, the unrolling algorithm is one of the most popular
due to the synergistic integration of traditional model-based reconstruction
methods and modern neural networks, providing an interpretable and highly
accurate reconstruction. However, when the sensing operator is highly
ill-posed, gradient steps on the data-fidelity term can hinder convergence and
degrade reconstruction quality. To address this issue, we propose UTOPY, a
homotopy continuation formulation for training the unrolling algorithm. Mainly,
this method involves using a well-posed (synthetic) sensing matrix at the
beginning of the unrolling network optimization. We define a continuation path
strategy to transition smoothly from the synthetic fidelity to the desired
ill-posed problem. This strategy enables the network to progressively
transition from a simpler, well-posed inverse problem to the more challenging
target scenario. We theoretically show that, for projected gradient
descent-like unrolling models, the proposed continuation strategy generates a
smooth path of unrolling solutions. Experiments on compressive sensing and
image deblurring demonstrate that our method consistently surpasses
conventional unrolled training, achieving up to 2.5 dB PSNR improvement in
reconstruction performance. Source code at

</details>


### [228] [Subjective Evaluation of Low Distortion Coded Light Fields with View Synthesis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.14761)
*Daniela Saraiva,Joao Prazeres,Manuela Pereira,Antonio M. G. Pinheiro*

Main category: eess.IV

TL;DR: 本文对视点合成对光场压缩的影响进行了主观分析，使用JPEG AIC-3测试方法评估质量，并基于主观结果验证了一系列指标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 光场技术产生大量数据，需要高效压缩。视点合成在光场技术中扮演关键角色，但其与压缩的相互作用尚未被充分探索。

Method: 首先，通过删除原始光场的视点来创建稀疏采样光场。然后，使用JPEG Pleno和VVC对原始光场和采样光场进行编码。接着，对压缩后的采样光场应用视点合成以重建与原始光场相同数量的视点。主观评估遵循JPEG AIC-3测试方法，该方法通过并排闪烁测试来评估图像质量。最后，使用这些主观结果来验证一系列指标。

Result: 通过JPEG AIC-3测试方法获得了主观评估结果，这些结果被用于验证一系列选定的指标。

Conclusion: 本研究对视点合成在光场压缩中的作用进行了主观分析，并利用获得的主观结果验证了相关质量评估指标。

Abstract: Light field technology is a powerful imaging method that captures both the
intensity and direction of light rays in a scene, enabling the reconstruction
of 3D information and supporting a range of unique applications. However, light
fields produce vast amounts of data, making efficient compression essential for
their practical use. View synthesis plays a key role in light field technology
by enabling the generation of new views, yet its interaction with compression
has not been fully explored. In this work, a subjective analysis of the effect
of view synthesis on light field compression is conducted. To achieve this, a
sparsely sampled light field is created by dropping views from an original
light field. Both light fields are then encoded using JPEG Pleno and VVC. View
synthesis is then applied to the compressed sampled light field to reconstruct
the same number of views as the original. The subjective evaluation follows the
proposed JPEG AIC-3 test methodology designed to assess the quality of
high-fidelity compressed images. This test consists of two test stimuli
displayed side-by-side, each alternating between an original and a coded view,
creating a flicker effect on both sides. The user must choose which side has
the stronger flicker and, therefore, the lower quality. Using these subjective
results, a selection of metrics is validated.

</details>


### [229] [Hint: hierarchical inter-frame correlation for one-shot point cloud sequence compression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.14859)
*Yuchen Gao,Qi Zhang*

Main category: eess.IV

TL;DR: HINT是一种利用时空关联进行序列点云压缩的方法，显著降低了解码延迟并提高了压缩效率，相较于G-PCC有数十倍的加速和高达43.6%的比特率降低。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有深度学习点云压缩方法，特别是那些依赖父/兄弟上下文和逐层自回归的方法，存在10到100秒的解码延迟问题，限制了其实用性。

Method: 该论文提出了HINT方法，通过整合时空关联进行序列点云压缩。具体而言，它采用两阶段时间特征提取（父级存在图和子级上一帧邻域查找），将这些时间线索与空间特征通过逐元素相加融合，并采用分组策略进行编码。

Result: HINT实现了105毫秒的编码时间和140毫秒的解码时间，分别比G-PCC加速了49.6倍和21.6倍，同时比特率降低高达43.6%。此外，它持续优于强大的纯空间基线RENO。

Conclusion: HINT通过有效整合时空关联，显著降低了序列点云压缩的解码延迟，并大幅提高了压缩效率，在性能上超越了现有方法。

Abstract: Deep learning has demonstrated strong capability in compressing point clouds.
Within this area, entropy modeling for lossless compression is widely
investigated. However, most methods rely solely on parent orsibling contexts
and level-wise autoregression, which suffers from decoding latency on the order
of 10 to 100 seconds. We propose HINT, a method that integrates temporal and
spatial correlation for sequential point cloud compression. Specifically, it
first uses a two stage temporal feature extraction: (i) a parent-level
existence map and (ii) a child-level neighborhood lookup in the previous frame.
These cues are fused with the spatial features via elementwise addition and
encoded with a group-wise strategy. Experimental results show that HINT
achieves encoding and decoding time at 105 ms and 140 ms, respectively,
equivalent to 49.6x and 21.6x acceleration in comparison with G-PCC, while
achieving up to bit rate reduction of 43.6%, in addition, consistently
outperforming over the strong spatial only baseline (RENO).

</details>


### [230] [Undersampled Phase Retrieval with Image Priors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.15026)
*Stanislas Ducotterd,Zhiyuan Hu,Michael Unser,Jonathan Dong*

Main category: eess.IV

TL;DR: 该研究表明，在欠采样严重的结构化随机傅里叶测量下，图像先验显著改善了相位恢复的重建质量，甚至低于弱恢复阈值也能实现准确重建。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 相位恢复是一个具有挑战性的非线性逆问题，旨在从仅有幅度的测量中恢复复杂信号。现有理论和算法通常忽略信号先验，而本研究旨在评估图像先验在此类问题中的有效性。

Method: 在严重欠采样和结构化随机傅里叶测量背景下，评估了多种图像先验对相位恢复重建性能的影响。

Result: 图像先验显著提高了重建质量，即使在低于弱恢复阈值的情况下也能实现准确重建。

Conclusion: 利用图像先验对于从仅有幅度的测量中恢复复杂信号（相位恢复）至关重要，尤其是在测量条件极具挑战性（如严重欠采样）时，能够大幅提升重建性能。

Abstract: Phase retrieval seeks to recover a complex signal from amplitude-only
measurements, a challenging nonlinear inverse problem. Current theory and
algorithms often ignore signal priors. By contrast, we evaluate here a variety
of image priors in the context of severe undersampling with structured random
Fourier measurements. Our results show that those priors significantly improve
reconstruction, allowing accurate reconstruction even below the weak recovery
threshold.

</details>


### [231] [Learning Mechanistic Subtypes of Neurodegeneration with a Physics-Informed Variational Autoencoder Mixture Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.15124)
*Sanduni Pinnawala,Annabelle Hartanto,Ivor J. A. Simpson,Peter A. Wijeratne*

Main category: eess.IV

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种深度生成模型，将反应扩散偏微分方程（PDEs）整合到变分自编码器（VAE）混合模型框架中，以学习由物理驱动的潜在动态模型混合体。该方法旨在从神经影像数据中推断神经退行性疾病（如阿尔茨海默病）的机制亚型，克服了传统单一PDE模型的局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 建模神经退行性疾病的潜在机制需要能够从稀疏、高维神经影像数据中捕获异质和空间变化的动态。现有的物理集成机器学习方法仅限于考虑单个PDE，这严重限制了它们在具有多种机制和亚型的疾病中的应用，并导致模型错误指定和退化问题。

Method: 本文提出了一种深度生成模型，用于学习由基于物理的PDEs控制的潜在动态模型混合体。该方法将反应扩散PDEs集成到变分自编码器（VAE）混合模型框架中，支持从神经影像数据中推断可解释潜在变量（例如扩散率和反应速率）的亚型。

Result: 该方法在合成基准上进行了评估，并展示了其从正电子发射断层扫描（PET）数据中揭示阿尔茨海默病进展机制亚型的潜力。

Conclusion: 该研究通过整合多个物理驱动的PDEs到VAE混合模型中，成功地为建模神经退行性疾病提供了更具解释性和实用性的方法，能够识别疾病的机制亚型，克服了现有单一PDE方法的局限性。

Abstract: Modelling the underlying mechanisms of neurodegenerative diseases demands
methods that capture heterogeneous and spatially varying dynamics from sparse,
high-dimensional neuroimaging data. Integrating partial differential equation
(PDE) based physics knowledge with machine learning provides enhanced
interpretability and utility over classic numerical methods. However, current
physics-integrated machine learning methods are limited to considering a single
PDE, severely limiting their application to diseases where multiple mechanisms
are responsible for different groups (i.e., subtypes) and aggravating problems
with model misspecification and degeneracy. Here, we present a deep generative
model for learning mixtures of latent dynamic models governed by physics-based
PDEs, going beyond traditional approaches that assume a single PDE structure.
Our method integrates reaction-diffusion PDEs within a variational autoencoder
(VAE) mixture model framework, supporting inference of subtypes of
interpretable latent variables (e.g. diffusivity and reaction rates) from
neuroimaging data. We evaluate our method on synthetic benchmarks and
demonstrate its potential for uncovering mechanistic subtypes of Alzheimer's
disease progression from positron emission tomography (PET) data.

</details>
